Edit `server/prisma/schema.prisma` with your changes (add columns, new enums, etc.)\n+\n+// turbo\n+2. Create a safe migration (preserves all existing data):\n+```powershell\n+cd server\n+npx prisma migrate dev --name describe_your_change_here\n+```\n+Example: `npx prisma migrate dev --name add_notes_to_leave_request`\n+\n+// turbo\n+3. Regenerate the Prisma client:\n+```powershell\n+npx prisma generate\n+```\n+*Tip: If you get an EPERM error, stop any running `npm run dev` servers first.*\n+\n+4. Restart the dev server if it didn't auto-restart:\n+```powershell\n+# The nodemon watcher usually handles this automatically\n+```\n+\n+## For Production Deployments\n+\n+// turbo\n+Run only migrations that haven't been applied yet (safe, non-destructive):\n+```powershell\n+cd server\n+npx prisma migrate deploy\n+```\n+\n+## Backup Before Any Schema Change (Recommended)\n+\n+Run the existing backup script first:\n+```powershell\n+cd server\n+.\\backup-database.bat\n+```\n+\n+## What Each Command Does\n+\n+| Command | Safe? | What it does |\n+|---|---|---|\n+| `prisma migrate dev --name X` | ✅ YES | Creates migration file + applies it, data preserved |\n+| `prisma migrate deploy` | ✅ YES | Applies pending migrations only, used in production |\n+| `prisma generate` | ✅ YES | Regenerates the TypeScript client, no DB changes |\n+| `prisma db push` | ⚠️ RISKY | Forces schema onto DB, can drop data on enum changes |\n+| `prisma migrate reset` | ❌ NO | Drops everything and reruns all migrations from scratch |\n+| `ts-node src/scripts/reset-db.ts --confirm` | ❌ NO | Deletes all rows, only for fresh dev setup |\ndiff --git a/.env b/.env\ndeleted file mode 100644\nindex 377b2c0..0000000\n--- a/.env\n+++ /dev/null\n@@ -1 +0,0 @@\n-VITE_API_URL=http://localhost:5000/api\ndiff --git a/.env.production b/.env.production\ndeleted file mode 100644\nindex e9e3bf0..0000000\n--- a/.env.production\n+++ /dev/null\n@@ -1 +0,0 @@\n-VITE_API_URL=http://YOUR_SERVER_PUBLIC_IP:5000/api\ndiff --git a/.gitignore b/.gitignore\nindex a547bf3..fde6e45 100644\n--- a/.gitignore\n+++ b/.gitignore\n@@ -12,6 +12,11 @@ dist\n dist-ssr\n *.local\n \n+# Environment files - NEVER commit secrets\n+.env\n+.env.*\n+!.env.example\n+\n # Editor directories and files\n .vscode/*\n !.vscode/extensions.json\ndiff --git a/AUDIT_REPORT.md b/AUDIT_REPORT.md\nnew file mode 100644\nindex 0000000..1b8ed66\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/AUDIT_REPORT.md\n@@ -0,0 +1,53 @@\n+# 🏥 Production Audit Report: Leave Tracker\n+\n+This report summarizes the audit checks performed on the Leave Tracker application based on professional software engineering standards.\n+\n+## 1. 🔐 Security Audit\n+| Check | Status | Action Taken |\n+|---|---|---|\n+| Authentication \u0026 Authorization | ✅ Passed | Confirmed RBAC logic for OM/GM/CEO roles. |\n+| SQL Injection | ✅ Passed | Prisma ORM uses parameterized queries by default. creates leave request from phone → Email sent to OM → Request not visible in employee's profile on any device\n+\n+**Root Cause**: Query cache invalidation mismatch - the invalidation key didn't match the actual query key parameters\n+\n+**Solution**: Implemented comprehensive cache clearing and forced refetch after submission\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🔧 Changes Made\n+\n+### 1. **Fixed Query Invalidation** (`src/pages/Requests.tsx`)\n+\n+**Before:**\n+```typescript\n+queryClient.invalidateQueries({ queryKey: ['leaveRequests'] });\n+```\n+**Problem**: Query uses `['leaveRequests', currentPage, itemsPerPage, user?.role]`, so simple invalidation didn't clear the cache.\n+\n+**After:**\n+```typescript\n+// Clear ALL leave request caches (important for cross-device sync)\n+queryClient.removeQueries({ queryKey: ['leaveRequests'] });\n+\n+// Force immediate refetch with current parameters\n+await queryClient.refetchQueries({ \n+  queryKey: ['leaveRequests', currentPage, itemsPerPage, user?.role],\n+  type: 'active'\n+});\n+```\n+\n+### 2. **Disabled Query Caching for Fresh Data**\n+\n+```typescript\n+const { data: paginatedData, isLoading } = useQuery({\n+  queryKey: ['leaveRequests', currentPage, itemsPerPage, user?.role],\n+  queryFn: async ({ signal }) =\u003e { /* ... */ },\n+  enabled: !!user,\n+  staleTime: 0,  // ⭐ Always refetch on mount\n+  gcTime: 0,     // ⭐ Don't cache (ensures cross-device sync)\n+});\n+```\n+\n+**Why this matters**:\n+- `staleTime: 0` ensures data is always considered stale, triggering refetch on page load\n+- `gcTime: 0` prevents React Query from keeping data in memory cache\n+- Critical for multi-device scenarios where cached data could be outdated\n+\n+### 3. **Added Comprehensive Logging**\n+\n+```typescript\n+console.log('✅ Leave request submitted successfully');\n+console.log('📊 Current user role:', user?.role);\n+console.log('📱 Invalidating queries and forcing refetch...');\n+// ... submission logic\n+console.log('✅ Queries refreshed - request should now be visible');\n+```\n+\n+```typescript\n+console.log(`📥 Fetching leave requests for ${user?.role} from ${endpoint}`);\n+// ... API call\n+console.log(`✅ Received ${response.data.data.leaveRequests.length} leave requests`);\n+```\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🧪 How to Verify the Fix\n+\n+### Test Scenario 1: Submit from Phone, View on PC\n+\n+1. **On Phone** (connected to same WiFi):\n+   ```\n+   a. Navigate to http://192.168.1.5:8080\n+   b. Login as employee\n+   c. Create new leave request\n+   d. Submit\n+   e. Check browser console (enable remote debugging):\n+      ✅ \"Leave request submitted successfully\"\n+      ✅ \"Queries refreshed - request should now be visible\"\n+   ```\n+\n+2. **On PC** (same or different):\n+   ```\n+   a. Open http://localhost:8080 or http://192.168.1.5:8080\n+   b. Login as same employee\n+   c. Navigate to \"Requests\" page\n+   d. Check browser console:\n+      📥 \"Fetching leave requests for EMPLOYEE from /leave-requests/my-leaves\"\n+      ✅ \"Received 1 leave requests\" (includes newly created request)\n+   e. Request should be visible in the list\n+   ```\n+\n+### Test Scenario 2: Submit from PC, View on Phone\n+\n+1. **On PC**:\n+   ```\n+   a. Submit leave request\n+   b. Console should show cache clearing and refetch\n+   ```\n+\n+2. **On Phone**:\n+   ```\n+   a. Navigate to Requests page\n+   b. Request appears immediately (no cache, fresh fetch)\n+   ```\n+\n+### Test Scenario 3: Rapid Switching Between Devices\n+\n+1. Create request on Device A\n+2. Immediately switch to Device B\n+3. Navigate to Requests page\n+4. Should see the new request (staleTime: 0 forces refetch)\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📊 How It Works Now\n+\n+### Request Submission Flow\n+\n+```\n+┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│  1. Employee submits request (any device)              │\n+│     - POST /leave-requests                             │\n+└────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘\n+                     ↓\n+┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│  2. Backend saves to database                          │\n+│     - Creates LeaveRequest record                      │\n+│     - Status: PENDING_OM                               │\n+│     - Sends email to Operations Managers               │\n+└────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘\n+                     ↓\n+┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│ 3. Frontend clears ALL cached leave request queries   │\n+│     queryClient.removeQueries(['leaveRequests'])       │\n+└────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘\n+                     ↓\n+┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│  4. Frontend forces immediate refetch                  │\n+│     - GET /leave-requests/my-leaves (for employee)     │\n+│     - Includes newly created request                   │\n+└────────────────────┬───────────────────────────────────┘\n+                     ↓\n+┌────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│  5. Request appears in employee's list                 │\n+│     ✅ Visible on submission device                    │\n+│     ✅ Visible on all other devices (staleTime: 0)     │\n+└────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n+```\n+\n+### Cross-Device Data Synchronization\n+\n+**Device A (Phone)**:\n+```\n+1. Submit request\n+2. queryClient.removeQueries() clears cache\n+3. Immediate refetch shows new request\n+```\n+\n+**Device B (Laptop)** - Seconds later:\n+```\n+1. User navigates to Requests page\n+2. staleTime: 0 → triggers fresh fetch (ignores any cache)\n+3. GET /leave-requests/my-leaves\n+4. Receives ALL requests including new one\n+5. Displays complete list\n+```\n+\n+**Device C (Tablet)** - Minutes later:\n+```\n+1. User opens Requests page\n+2. gcTime: 0 → no memory cache exists\n+3. Fresh fetch from database\n+4. All requests visible\n+```\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🔍 Debugging Commands\n+\n+### Browser Console (F12) on Any Device\n+\n+After submitting a request, you should see:\n+```\n+✅ Leave request submitted successfully\n+📊 Current user role: EMPLOYEE\n+📱 Invalidating queries and forcing refetch...\n+📥 Fetching leave requests for EMPLOYEE from /leave-requests/my-leaves\n+✅ Received 1 leave requests\n+✅ Queries refreshed - Clear cache on the problematic device\n+2. Perform hard refresh (Ctrl + F5)\n+3. Check if using same user account\n+4. Verify network connection (same WiFi)\n+```\n+\n+### Issue: Request appears after page refresh but not immediately\n+\n+**This is expected behavior now** - With `staleTime: 0`, navigating to the page triggers a fresh fetch. The submission itself also forces an immediate refetch.\n+\n+If it still doesn't appear:\n+1. Check browser console for errors\n+2. Verify API response in Network tab\n+3. Leave Request Approval System\n+\n+## 🎯 Quick Start for Executives (OM, GM, CEO)\n+\n+This guide explains how to approve or reject leave requests from **any device** on your corporate network - whether you're on your office desktop, laptop at home (on same network), tablet, or phone.\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📱 Accessing the System\n+\n+### From the Server PC (Local Access)\n+Open your browser and navigate to:\n+```\n+http://localhost:8080\n+```\n+\n+### From ANY Other Device on the Network\n+1. **Find the Server IP Address** - Ask your IT administrator or check the server startup logs\n+2. **Open your browser** on your device (laptop, phone, tablet)\n+3. **Navigate to**:\n+   ```\n+   http://[SERVER_IP]:8080\n+   ```\n+   Example: `http://192.168.1.5:8080`\n+\n+4. **Login** with your credentials:\n+   - **Email**: Your company email address\n+   - **Password**: Your phone number (or custom password if changed)\n+\n+---\n+\n+## ✅ Approving Leave Requests\n+\n+### Operations Manager (OM) - Phase 1 Approval\n+\n+**Role**: First-level approval for all leave requests\n+\n+**Steps**:\n+1. Login to the system\n+2. Navigate to **\"Requests\"** from the sidebar\n+3. You'll see all pending requests marked as `PENDING_OM`\n+4. For each request:\n+   - **Click to expand** and view full details (dates, reason, handover notes)\n+   - Review employee's leave balance\n+   - Check scattered dates if applicable\n+5. **To Approve**:\n+   - Click the **\"Approve (OM)\"** button\n+   - Request automatically moves to `PENDING_GM` status\n+   - GM receives email notification\n+6. **To Reject**:\n+   - Click the **\"Reject\"** button\n+   - Provide a mandatory reason\n+   - Employee receives notification\n+\n+**Bulk Actions**: Select multiple requests using checkboxes and click **\"Approve Selected\"** or **\"Reject Selected\"**\n+\n+---\n+\n+### General Manager (GM) - Phase 2 Approval\n+\n+**Role**: Second-level approval for OM-endorsed requests\n+\n+**Steps**:\n+1. Login to the system\n+2. Navigate to **\"Requests\"**\n+3. Look for requests with status `PENDING_GM`\n+4. Review:\n+   - Employee details and leave history\n+   - OM's endorsement\n+   - Department impact\n+5. **To Approve**:\n+   - Click **\"Approve (GM)\"** button\n+   - System notifies: \"Request approved (GM). Pending manual CEO signature.\"\n+   - CEO can now provide final signature\n+6. **To Reject**:\n+   - Click **\"Reject\"** button\n+   - Provide detailed reason\n+   - Request marked as `REJECTED_GM`\n+\n+---\n+\n+### Chief Executive Officer (CEO) - Final Approval\n+\n+**Role**: Final signature on GM-approved requests\n+\n+**Steps**:\n+1. Login to the system\n+2. Navigate to **\"Requests\"**\n+3. Filter to show requests at `PENDING_CEO` status (or check your email for notifications)\n+4. Review the full approval chain:\n+   - Employee signature ✓\n+   - OM approval ✓\n+   - GM approval ✓\n+5. **To Finalize Approval**:\n+   - Click **\"Approve (CEO)\"** button\n+   - Request status changes to `APPROVED`\n+   - Employee receives final confirmation\n+   - Leave is now official and appears on the calendar\n+\n+**Alternative**: Download the PDF, sign manually, and upload (if preferred)\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📧 Email Notifications\n+\n+All approvers receive **real-time email notifications** when:\n+- ✉️ A new request enters their approval queue\n+- ✉️ A request they approved moves to the next phase\n+- ✉️ A request is rejected by any approver\n+\n+**Email Links Work from Any Device**: Click the **\"Review \u0026 Process Request\"** button in the email, and you'll be taken directly to the system - **even from your phone or tablet!**\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📊 Dashboard Features for Executives\n+\n+### Operations Manager Dashboard\n+- **Pending OM Requests**: Count of requests awaiting your approval\n+- **Approved by OM**: Requests you've endorsed\n+- **Team Analytics**: Department-wise leave trends\n+- **Quick Actions**: Approve multiple requests at once\n+\n+### General Manager Dashboard  \n+- **Pending GM Approvals**: Requests endorsed by OM\n+- **Department Overview**: Leave distribution across teams\n+- **Monthly Trends**: Visual charts of leave patterns\n+- **Reports Access**: Detailed analytics and PDF exports\n+\n+### CEO Dashboard\n+- **Final Approvals**: Requests awaiting CEO signature\n+- **Company-wide Statistics**: Total employees, active leaves\n+- **Executive Reports**: High-level analytics\n+- **Audit Logs**: Complete approval history\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🔐 Security \u0026 Permissions\n+\n+### Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)\n+- **Operations Managers** can:\n+  - View all employee leave requests\n+  - Provide first-level approval\n+  - Reject requests with reasons\n+  - Access team calendars and reports\n+  \n+- **General Managers** can:\n+  - All OM permissions +\n+  - Provide second-level approval\n+  - Override OM decisions\n+  - Access advanced analytics\n+  \n+- **CEO** can:\n+  - All permissions +\n+  - Provide final signature\n+  - Access complete audit trail\n+  - Manage system settings\n+\n+### Network Security\n+- System uses **JWT tokens** for authentication\n+- Sessions are secure and device-specific\n+- Automatic logout on inactivity\n+- All API requests require valid authorization\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🎯 Best Practices\n+\n+### For Quick Approvals\n+1. **Enable Email Notifications** - Get instant alerts on new requests\n+2. **Use Bulk Actions** - Approve multiple routine requests together\n+3. **Check Dashboard Daily** - See pending counts at a glance\n+4. **Review Handover Notes** - Ensure continuity of operations\n+\n+### For Mobile/Tablet Use\n+1. **Bookmark the URL** - Save the server IP address for quick access\n+2. **Portrait Mode Works Best** - UI is optimized for mobile viewing\n+3. **Use Full Details View** - Tap a request to see complete information\n+4. **Approve in Two Taps** - Open request → Approve button\n+\n+### For Remote Work (Same Network)\n+1. **Connect to VPN** (if accessing from home on company network extension)\n+2. **Use Same IP Address** - `http://192.168.x.x:8080`\n+3. **Check Email Links** - They automatically point to the correct IP\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🆘 Troubleshooting\n+\n+### \"Cannot approve - button disabled\"\n+**Solution**: Check if the request is in the correct status for your role:\n+- OM can only approve `PENDING_OM`\n+- GM can only approve `PENDING_GM`  \n+- CEO can only approve requests with GM approval\n+\n+### \"Cannot connect to system from my device\"\n+**Solutions**:\n+1. Verify you're on the same network as the server\n+2. Check the IP address is correct (match to server logs)\n+3. Try `http://` (not `https://`)\n+4. Clear browser cache and retry\n+5. Check Windows Firewall settings on server PC\n+\n+### \"Login successful but redirects to login page\"\n+**Solutions**:\n+1. Clear browser cache and cookies\n+2. Check browser console (F12) for API URL\n+3. Verify backend is running on server PC\n+4. Try from a different browser\n+\n+### \"Email link doesn't work\"\n+**Solutions**:\n+1. Copy the URL from email\n+2. Paste into browser address bar\n+3. Ensure you're on the same network\n+4. Login if session expired\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📞 IT Support Information\n+\n+**System Requirements**:\n+- Modern web browser (Chrome, Edge, Firefox, Safari)\n+- Network connectivity to server PC\n+- Ports 5000 (Backend API) and 8080 (Frontend) accessible\n+\n+**Server Information** (from startup logs):\n+```\n+============================================================\n+🚀 AlanDick Leave Tracker Server Started\n+============================================================\n+📍 Local Access:   http://localhost:5000\n+🌐 Network Access: http://192.168.1.5:5000\n+📧 Email Links:    http://192.168.1.5:8080\n+============================================================\n+```\n+\n+**For Assistance**:\n+- Contact your IT Administrator\n+- Reference: `NETWORK_CONFIG.md` for technical setup\n+- Check server logs for connectivity diagnostics\n+\n+---\n+\n+## ✨ Pro Tips\n+\n+1. **Keyboard Shortcuts**: Navigate with Tab, approve with Enter\n+2. **Filter by Status**: Use the status dropdown to focus on your pending queue\n+3. **Calendar View**: Check the calendar to see team leave patterns before approving\n+4. **Download PDFs**: Export approval documents for record-keeping\n+5. **Audit Trail**: All approvals are logged with timestamp and approver details\n+\n+---\n+\n+**Questions?** Contact your system administrator or HR department.\n+\n+**Last Updated**: 2026-02-17  \n+**System Version**: Leave Tracker v1.0  \n+**AlanDick \u0026 Company (East Africa) Ltd**\ndiff --git a/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.txt b/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.txt\nnew file mode 100644\nindex 0000000..777cef2\n--- /dev/null\n+++ b/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.txt\n@@ -0,0 +1,266 @@\n+┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│                                                                          │\n+│  ✅  EXECUTIVE APPROVAL FROM ANY DEVICE - Access Configuration\n+\n+This Leave Tracker system is designed to work seamlessly across your local network, enabling access from multiple devices using the server's IP address.\n+\n+### How It Works\n+\n+#### 1. **Dynamic IP Detection**\n+The system automatically detects the server's network IP address on startup and uses it for:\n+- Email notification links\n+- Cross-device API communication\n+- Frontend-to-backend connectivity\n+\n+#### 2. **Frontend (Port 8080)**\n+- **Vite Dev Server** listens on `::` (all IPv6/IPv4 interfaces) via `vite --host`\n+- **Dynamic API Detection** in `src/lib/api.ts` automatically uses the browser's current hostname\n+- Supports access via:\n+  - `http://localhost:8080` (local machine)\n+  - `http://[SERVER_IP]:8080` (network devices)\n+\n+#### 3. **Backend (Port 5000)**\n+- **Express Server** binds to `0.0.0.0` (all network interfaces)\n+- Accepts connections from any device on the same network\n+- CORS configured to accept requests from any origin\n+\n+#### 4. **Email Links**\n+All system-generated emails (welcome, leave requests, approvals) automatically include:\n+- Primary link: Server IP address (e.g., `http://192.168.1.5:8080`)\n+- Fallback link: Localhost (for server machine access)\n+\n+### Server Startup Information\n+\n+When you start the backend, you'll see:\n+```\n+============================================================\n+🚀 AlanDick Leave Tracker Server Started\n+============================================================\n+Server running on port 5000\n+📍 Local Access:   http://localhost:5000\n+🌐 Network Access: http://192.168.1.5:5000\n+📧 Email Links:    http://192.168.1.5:8080\n+============================================================\n+```\n+\n+Use the **Network Access** URL to access from other devices on the same WiFi/LAN.\n+\n+### Accessing from Other Devices\n+\n+1. **Find the Server IP**: Check the backend startup logs for the \"Network Access\" URL\n+2. **Open Browser**: On any device connected to the same network, navigate to:\n+   - `http://[SERVER_IP]:8080` (Frontend)\n+3. **Login**: Use your credentials as normal\n+\n+### Troubleshooting\n+\n+#### Can't connect from another device?\n+1. **Firewall**: Ensure Windows Firewall allows ports 5000 and 8080\n+   ```powershell\n+   # Run PowerShell as Administrator\n+   New-NetFirewallRule -DisplayName \"Leave Tracker Frontend\" -Direction Inbound -Protocol TCP -LocalPort 8080 -Action Allow\n+   New-NetFirewallRule -DisplayName \"Leave Tracker Backend\" -Direction Inbound -Protocol TCP -LocalPort 5000 -Action Allow\n+   ```\n+\n+2. **Network**: Verify both devices are on the same network (same WiFi/Ethernet segment)\n+\n+3. **Check API URL**: Open browser console (F12) on the client device and look for:\n+   ```\n+   📡 API Base URL detected: http://[IP]:5000/api\n+   ```\n+\n+#### Login loops or authentication issues?\n+- Clear browser cache and localStorage\n+- Verify the API URL logged in console matches the server IP\n+- Restart both frontend and backend servers\n+\n+### Architecture Summary\n+\n+```\n+┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│  Device 1 (Server PC)                           │\n+│  ├─ Frontend (Vite)     → 0.0.0.0:8080         │\n+│  └─ Backend (Express)   → 0.0.0.0:5000         │\n+└─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n+            ↕ (LAN/WiFi Network)\n+┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│  Device 2 (Phone/Tablet/PC)                     │\n+│  └─ Browser → http://192.168.1.5:8080          │\n+│     └─ Auto-detects API → http://192.168.1.5:5000 │\n+└─────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n+```\n+\n+### Key Files Modified for IP Support\n+\n+1. **`server/src/server.ts`**: Binds to `0.0.0.0`, displays network IP on startup\n+2. **`server/src/app.ts`**: Enhanced CORS configuration for cross-origin requests\n+3. **`server/src/services/email.service.ts`**: Uses detected server IP in all email links\n+4. **`src/lib/api.ts`**: Dynamic API URL based on browser hostname\n+5. **`vite.config.ts`**: Server listens on all interfaces\n+6. **`package.json`**: Frontend dev script uses `vite --host`\n+\n+---\n+\n+**💡 Tip**: Bookmark the server IP URL on your mobile devices for quick access!\ndiff --git a/PDF_FIXES_SUMMARY.txt b/PDF_FIXES_SUMMARY.txt\nnew file mode 100644\nindex Excessive vertical spacing (`mt-12`, `pt-8`, `space-y-8`)\n+2. Large signature block heights (`min-h-[60px]`)\n+3. Excessive padding (`p-6`, `gap-12`)\n+4. Verbose footer with multiple lines of text\n+\n+### **Issue 2: White Container Around Logo**\n+**Problem**: Logo had unnecessary white background container (`bg-white/95 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg`) making it look boxed and unprofessional.\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🔧 Changes Made\n+\n+### **1. Logo - Removed White Container**\n+\n+**Before**:\n+```tsx\n+\u003cimg\n+  src=\"/company-logo.jpg\"\n+  alt=\"Company Logo\"\n+  className=\"h-16 w-auto object-contain bg-white/95 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg flex-shrink-0\"\n+/\u003e\n+```\n+**Issues**:\n+- `bg-white/95` = White background box around logo\n+- `px-4 py-2` = Extra padding creating a container effect\n+- `rounded-lg` = Rounded corners on container\n+- `shadow-lg` = Drop shadow on container\n+\n+**After**:\n+```tsx\n+\u003cimg\n+  src=\"/company-logo.jpg\"\n+  alt=\"Company Logo\"\n+  className=\"h-16 w-auto object-contain flex-shrink-0\"\n+/\u003e\n+```\n+**Result**: ✅ Logo displays independently without container, cleaner professional look!\n+\n+---\n+\n+### **2. Footer - Compact Corporate Design**\n+\n+**Before** (Verbose, 4+ lines, excessive spacing):\n+```tsx\n+\u003cdiv className=\"mt-12 pt-8 border-t border-slate-200 text-center\"\u003e\n+  \u003cdiv className=\"inline-block px-10 py-2 border-x border-[#08033F] text-[10px] font-bold text-[#08033F] uppercase tracking-[0.3em] mb-4\"\u003e\n+    Official Communication\n+  \u003c/div\u003e\n+  \u003cp className=\"text-[9px] text-slate-400 leading-relaxed uppercase tracking-widest\"\u003e\n+    This document is a certified extract from the Leave Management System records.\n+    \u003cbr /\u003e\n+    Generated on {date with time} by System Administrator\n+  \u003c/p\u003e\n+\u003c/div\u003e\n+```\n+**Issues**:\n+- `mt-12` (48px top margin) - way too much!\n+- `pt-8` (32px top padding) - excessive\n+- Multi-line verbose text taking vertical space\n+- Center-aligned, taking more height\n+\n+**After** (Compact, single-line, corporate):\n+```tsx\n+\u003cdiv className=\"mt-6 pt-4 border-t-2 border-[#08033F]/10\"\u003e\n+  \u003cdiv className=\"flex items-center justify-between text-[8px] text-slate-500\"\u003e\n+    \u003cdiv className=\"flex items-center gap-2\"\u003e\n+      \u003cspan className=\"font-bold text-[#08033F]\"\u003e●\u003c/span\u003e\n+      \u003cspan className=\"uppercase tracking-wider\"\u003eOfficial Document\u003c/span\u003e\n+    \u003c/div\u003e\n+    \u003cdiv className=\"text-center\"\u003e\n+      \u003cspan className=\"font-semibold text-[#08033F] uppercase tracking-wide\"\u003eAlanDick \u0026 Company (East Africa) Ltd\u003c/span\u003e\n+    \u003c/div\u003e\n+    \u003cdiv className=\"text-right\"\u003e\n+      \u003cspan className=\"uppercase tracking-wider\"\u003e{short date}\u003c/span\u003e\n+    \u003c/div\u003e\n+  \u003c/div\u003e\n+\u003c/div\u003e\n+```\n+**Improvements**:\n+- ✅ `mt-6` (24px) - b/PDF_PRODUCTION_READY.md\n@@ -0,0 +1,393 @@\n+# 📄 Production-Ready PDF Generation - Improvements\n+\n+## ✅ Changes Made (Step Id: 1482)\n+\n+### **Issue 1: Logo Container Nesting**\n+**Problem**: The company logo was wrapped in an unnecessary `\u003cdiv className=\"flex-shrink-0\"\u003e` container, adding extra nesting and potential rendering issues in PDFs.\n+\n+**Before**:\n+```tsx\n+\u003cdiv className=\"flex-shrink-0\"\u003e\n+  \u003cimg\n+    src=\"/company-logo.jpg\"\n+    alt=\"Company Logo\"\n+    className=\"h-16 w-auto object-contain bg-white/95 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg\"\n+  /\u003e\n+\u003c/div\u003e\n+```\n+\n+**After**:\n+```tsx\n+\u003cimg\n+  src=\"/company-logo.jpg\"\n+  alt=\"Company Logo\"\n+  className=\"h-16 w-auto object-contain bg-white/95 px-4 py-2 rounded-lg shadow-lg flex-shrink-0\"\n+/\u003e\n+```\n+\n+**Result**: ✅ Logo renders directly without container nesting, reducing DOM complexity and improving PDF rendering accuracy.\n+\n+---\n+\n+### **Issue 2: Inconsistent Document Padding**\n+**Problem**: The PDF had inconsistent margins and no industry-standard padding, making it look unprofessional.\n+\n+**Before**:\n+```tsx\n+\u003cdiv className=\"space-y-0 pt-4\" ref={detailsRef} style={{ backgroundColor: '#F6F6F5' }}\u003e\n+  {/* Sections had mx-4 margins creating inconsistency */}\n+  \u003cdiv className=\"... mx-4\"\u003e...\u003c/div\u003e\n+  \u003cdiv className=\"... mx-10\"\u003e...\u003c/div\u003e\n+\u003c/div\u003e\n+```\n+\n+**After**:\n+```tsx\n+\u003cdiv className=\"space-y-0 pt-4\" ref={detailsRef} style={{ \n+  backgroundColor: '#F6F6F5',\n+  padding: '96px 72px',  // Industry standard: ~1 inch margins on all sides\n+  minHeight: '1056px'    // A4 page height at 96 DPI\n+}}\u003e\n+  {/* All sections now have consistent spacing, no mx-4 */}\n+  \u003cdiv className=\"...\"\u003e...\u003c/div\u003e\n+\u003c/div\u003e\n+```\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📐 Industry-Standard PDF Specifications\n+\n+### **Page Margins**\n+Our PDFs now follow **ISO 216 (A4 paper)** and **industry best practices**:\n+\n+| Specification | Value | Pixels (at 72 DPI) | Explanation |\n+|---------------|-------|---------------------|-------------|\n+| **Top Margin** | 1 inch | 72px | Standard business document margin |\n+| **Right Margin** | 1 inch | 72px | Allows for binding/hole punching |\n+| **Bottom Margin** | 1 inch | 72px | Prevents content cutoff when printing |\n+| **Left Margin** | 1 inch | 72px | Professional appearance, binding space |\n+| **Page Width** | 210mm | 816px at 96 DPI | A4 standard width |\n+| **Page Height** | 297mm | 1056px at 96 DPI | A4 standard height |\n+\n+### **Why 72px = 1 inch?**\n+- Computer screens typically use **72 DPI (Dots Per Inch)**\n+- Printers often use **300 DPI** or higher\n+- **1 inch = 2.54 cm = 25.4 mm = 72 points (PostScript)**\n+- Our padding of `96px` at **96 DPI** translates to **1 inch** when printed\n+\n+### **PDF Generation Settings**\n+```typescript\n+const pdf = new jsPDF({\n+  orientation: 'portrait',\n+  unit: 'mm',\n+  format: 'a4',        // A4 paper size (210mm × 297mm)\n+  compress: true,      // Reduces file size\n+});\n+```\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🎨 Visual Hierarchy Improvements\n+\n+### **Before (Issues)**\n+```\n+┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│ Header (inconsistent padding)      │ ← No standard margins\n+├─────────────────────────────────────┤\n+│  ┌─────────────────────────────┐   │ ← mx-4 (inconsistent)\n+│  │ Section A                   │   │\n+│  └─────────────────────────────┘   │\n+│    ┌───────────────────────────┐   │ ← mx-10 (different!)\n+│    │ Footer                    │   │\n+│    └───────────────────────────┘   │\n+└─────────────────────────────────────┘\n+```\n+\n+### **After (Industry Standard)**\n+```\n+┌───────────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│ ◄─────── 1\" (72px) ────────────────► │\n+│ ▼                                         ▼\n+│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐\n+│ │ Header (full width edge-to-edge)   │ 1\" margin\n+│ ├─────────────────────────────────────┤\n+│ │                                      │\n+│ │ Section A (consistent padding)      │\n+│ │                                      │\n+│ ├─────────────────────────────────────┤\n+│ │                                      │\n+│ │ Section B (consistent padding)      │\n+│ │                                      │\n+│ ├─────────────────────────────────────┤\n+│ │                                      │\n+│ │ Footer (centered, consistent)       │\n+│ │                                      │\n+│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘\n+│ ▲                                         ▲\n+│ ◄─────── 1\" (72px) ────────────────►\n+└───────────────────────────────────────────┘\n+```\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 🔍 Detailed Changes by Section\n+\n+### **1. Main Container**\n+```tsx\n+// Main PDF container with industry-standard padding\n+style={{ \n+  backgroundColor: '#F6F6F5',\n+  padding: '96px 72px',  // Top/Bottom: 96px, Left/Right: 72px (~1 inch)\n+  minHeight: '1056px'    // Ensures full A4 page height\n+}}\n+```\n+\n+### **2. Header Section**\n+```tsx\n+// Header expands to edges using negative margins\n+style={{ \n+  backgroundColor: '#08033F',\n+  marginLeft: '-72px',    // Extends to left edge\n+  marginRight: '-72px',   // Extends to right edge\n+  marginTop: '-96px',     // Extends to top edge\n+  paddingLeft: '72px',    // Maintains content padding\n+  paddingRight: '72px',\n+  paddingTop: '40px',\n+  paddingBottom: '40px'\n+}}\n+```\n+**Result**: Header bar spans full width while content respects 1\" margins.\n+\n+### **3. Content Sections (A, B, C, D)**\n+**Before**: `className=\"... mx-4\"` (16px horizontal margin - inconsistent)\n+**After**: `className=\"...\"` (no extra margins - respects container padding)\n+\n+All sections now:\n+- ✅ Align perfectly with container padding\n+- ✅ Have consistent left/right edges\n+- ✅ Follow professional document layout standards\n+\n+### **4. Footer**\n+**Before**: `className=\"... mx-10\"` (40px margin - different from other sections!)\n+**After**: `className=\"...\"` (respects container padding)\n+\n+Footer now:\n+- ✅ Aligns with all other content\n+- ✅ Centered within the standard 1\" margins\n+- ✅ Professional appearance\n+\n+---\n+\n+## 📊 Comparison: Before vs After\n+\n+| Aspect | Before | After |\n+|--------|--------|-------|\n+| **Logo Nesting** | Wrapped in `\u003cdiv\u003e` | Direct `\u003cimg\u003e` tag with flex-shrink-0 |\n+| **Top Margin** | Variable (~4px) | Standard 1 inch (96px) |\n+| **Side Margins** | 16px (mx-4), 40px (mx-10) | Consistent 1 inch (72px) |\n+| **Bottom Margin** | Variable | Standard 1 inch (96px) |\n+| **Section Alignment** | Inconsistent | Perfectly aligned |\n+| **Print Quality** | Content may clip | Safe print area guaranteed |\n+| **Professional Look** | Amateur | Industry-standard |\n+| **Binding Space** | None | 1\" left margin (suitable for doc.setTextColor(...c);\n+}\n+\n+function fmtDate(d: string | null | undefined): string {\n+    if (!d) return '—';\n+    return new Date(d).toLocaleDateString('en-GB', { day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric' });\n+}\n+\n+/* ── Draw the common page footer ── */\n+function drawFooter(doc: jsPDF, pageNum: number, totalPages: number, docType: string) {\n+    const M = Date().toISOString()), PAGE.w - M, FOOTER_Y + 5, { align: 'right' });\n+\n+    // Separator line\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray, 'draw');\n+    doc.setLineWidth(0.15);\n+    doc.line(M, FOOTER_Y + 8, PAGE.w - M, FOOTER_Y + 8);\n+\n+    doc.setFontSize(6.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+    doc.text(`Page ${pageNum} of ${totalPages}  •  This document is system-generated and valid without physical signature where digitally approved.`, PAGE.w / 2, FOOTER_Y + 11, { align: 'center' });\n+}\n+\n+/* ── Draw the common page header with logo ── */\n+function drawHeader(doc: jsPDF, title: string, subtitle: string): number {\n+    const M = PAGE.marginX;\n+\n+    // Navy header bar\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(0, 0, PAGE.w, 28, 'F');\n+\n+    // Accent stripe\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(0, 28, PAGE.w, 1.5, 'F');\n+\n+    // Company logo (left)\n+    try {\n+        doc.addImage(COMPANY_LOGO_BASE64, 'JPEG', M, 5, 28, 18);\n+    } catch {\n+        // Fallback: text logo if image fails\n+        doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+        doc.setFontSize(10);\n+        setColor(doc, BRAND.white);\n+        doc.text('AD', M + 5, 16);\n+    }\n+\n+    // Title text (to the right of logo)\n+    const titleX = M + 34;\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(14);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.white);\n+    doc.text(title, titleX, 12);\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+    doc.setFontSize(8.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+    doc.text(subtitle, titleX, 18);\n+\n+    return 34; // y position after header\n+}\n+\n+\n+/* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n+     LEAVE REQUEST PDF  —  Two-page A4 corporate document\n+   ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */\n+\n+export interface LeaveRequestPdfData {\n+    id: string;\n+    employeeName: string;\n+    employeePosition: string;\n+              PAGE 1                             ║\n+       ║  Employee Info · Leave Details · Contact \u0026 Handover     ║\n+       ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝ doc.setFontSize(11);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.black);\n+    doc.text(`Submitted: ${fmtDate(req.submittedDate)}`, rx + 8, y + 18);\n+\n+    y += 26;\n+\n+    // Divider\n+    setColor(doc, doc.setFontSize(8);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+    doc.text('LEAVE PERIOD', M, y + 4);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(M, y + 6, 25, 0.6, 'F');\n+    y += 12;\n+\n+ doc.text('DURATION', x3 + 4, y + 5);\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(12);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.white);\n+    const durationText = `${req.days} Day${req.days !== 1 ? doc.text('REASON FOR LEAVE', M, y + 4);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(M, y + 6, 30, 0.6, 'F');\n+    y += 12;\n+\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.fieldBg, 'fill');\n+    const reasonLines = doc.splitTextToSize(req.reason || 'N/A', W - 16);\n+    // Limit reason lines so they don't overflow page 1\n+    const maxReasonLines = Math.min(reasonLines.length, 6);\n+    const BRAND.navy, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(M, y, 2.5, reasonH, 'F');\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'italic');\n+    doc.setFontSize(12);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.black);\n+    doc.text(clippedReasonLines, M + 8, y + 7);\n+\n+    y += reasonH + 8;\n+\n+    // Maximum y before footer zone on page 1\n+    const PAGE1_MAX_Y = FOOTER_Y - 6;\n+\n+    // ─── Divider ───\n+    if (y + 8 \u003c PAGE1_MAX_Y) {\n+        setColor(doc, BRAND.lightGray, 'draw');\n+        doc.setLineWidth(0.3);\n+        doc.line(M, y, PAGE.w - M, y);\n+        y += 8;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ─── Section: Contact \u0026 Handover ───\n+    if (y + 40 \u003c PAGE1_MAX_Y) {\n+        doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+        doc.setFontSize(8);\n+        setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+        doc.text('CONTACT \u0026 HANDOVER', M, y         { label: 'DEPARTMENT', value: req.handoverDepartment },\n+        ];\n+        const fW = (W - 9) / 4;\n+        const fH = 16;\n+        fields.forEach((f, i) =\u003e {\n+            const fx          setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+            doc.text(f.label, fx + 3, y + 5);\n+            doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+            doc.setFontSize(12);\n+            setColor(doc,       });\n+        y += fH + 6;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ─── Handover Report Details ───\n+    const handoverItems = [\n+        { label: 'BACKGROUND \u0026 WORK STATUS', value: req.handoverWorkStatus },\n+        { label: 'REQUIRED ACTIONS / FOLLOW UP', value: req.handoverActions },\n+        { label: 'STAKEHOLDER MANAGEMENT', value: req.handoverRelationships },\n+    ].filter(h =\u003e footer\n+            if (y + 18 \u003e PAGE1_MAX_Y) return;\n+\n+            setColor(doc, BRAND.fieldBg, 'fill');\n+            const lines = doc.splitTextToSize(item.value!, W - 16);\n+            // Limit lines to fit remaining space\n+            const availH = PAGE1_MAX_Y - y;\n+            const maxLines = Math.max(1, Math.floor((availH - 10) / 3.5));\n+            const clippedLines = BRAND.purpleGray, 'fill');\n+            doc.rect(M, y, 2, bH, 'F');\n+\n+            doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+            doc.setFontSize(5.5);\n+            setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+            doc.text(item.label, M + 7, y + 5);\n+\n+            doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+            doc.setFontSize(7.5);\n+            setColor(doc, BRAND.black);\n+            doc.text(clippedLines, M + 7, y + 10);\n+\n+            y += bH + 3;\n+        });\n+    }\n+\n+    // Page 1 footer removed as per request\n+\n+\n+    /* ╔══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗\n+       ║                      PAGE 2                             ║\n+       ║  Official Approval · Signatures · Status                ║\n+       ╚══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝ */\n+\n+    doc.addPage();\n+    y = drawHeader(doc, 'LEAVE APPLICATION FORM', 'ALANDICK \u0026 COMPANY (EAST AFRICA) LTD');\n+\n+    // ─── Compact summary reminder bar ───\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.fieldBg, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(M, y, W, 14, 'F');\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(M, y, 2.5, + 4);\n+    doc.text('TYPE', M + 145, y + 4);\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(9);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+    doc.text(req.employeeName, M + 8, y + 10);\n+ // Pending state — dashed border box\n+        setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray, 'draw');\n+        doc.setLineWidth(0.4);\n+        doc.setLineDashPattern([3, 3], 0);\n+        doc.rect(M, y, W, accentColor: BRAND.accentNavy,\n+        });\n+\n+        y += rowH * 3 + 10;\n+    }\n+\n+    // ─── Employee Signature Section ───\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(7.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+    doc.text('EMPLOYEE DECLARATION', M, y + 4);\n+    y += 10;\n+\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.fieldBg, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(M, y, W, 30, 'F');\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+    doc.setFontSize(12);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.black);\n+    doc.text('I hereby declare that the information provided above is accurate and complete to the best doc.setFontSize(6);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+    doc.text('Employee Signature', M + 6, y + 27);\n+    doc.text('Date', M + 100, y + 27);\n+\n+    y += 36;\n+\n+    // ─── Notes Section (optional extra space filler) ───\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(7.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+    doc.text('NOTES / ADDITIONAL COMMENTS', M, y + 4);\n+    y += 10;\n+\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.fieldBg, 'fill');\n+    const notesHeight = Math.max(30, FOOTER_Y - y - 20);\n+    doc.rect(M, y, W, notesHeight, 'F');\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.lightGray, 'draw');\n+    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);\n+    // Draw horizontal lines inside notes box\n+    for (let lineY = y + 8; lineY \u003c y + notesHeight - 2; lineY += 8) {\n+        doc.line(M + 4, lineY, M + `leave-request-${req.employeeName.replace(/\\s+/g, '-')}-${req.id.substring(0, 8)}.pdf`;\n+    doc.save(filename);\n+    return filename;\n+}\n+\n+\n+/* ── Helper: Draw one signature row ── */\n+function drawSignatureRow(\n+    doc: jsPDF,\n+    x: number, y: number,\n+    labelW: number, mainW: number, totalW: number, rowH: number,\n+    opts: {\n+        label: string;\n+        labelBg: [number, number, number];\n+        signatureName: string;\n+        signaturePresent: boolean;\n+        date: string;\n+        accentColor: [number, number, number];\n+    }\n+) {\n+    // Label column background\n+    setColor(doc, opts.labelBg, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(x, y, labelW, rowH, 'F');\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(6);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.white);\n+    const labelLines = opts.label.split('\\n');\n+    labelLines.forEach((line, i) =\u003e {\n+        doc.text(line.trim(), x + 4, y + 9 + i * 4);\n+    });\n+\n+    // Signature column\n+    const sigX = x + labelW;\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+    doc.setFontSize(5.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+    doc.text('SIGNATURE', sigX + 4, y + 5);\n+\n+    if (opts.signaturePresent) {\n+        doc.setFont('times', 'bolditalic');\n+        doc.setFontSize(14);\n+        setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+        doc.text(opts.signatureName, sigX + 4, y + 15);\n+    } else {\n+        // Dashed line placeholder\n+        setColor(doc, BRAND.lightGray, 'draw');\n+        doc.setLineWidth(0.25);\n+        doc.setLineDashPattern([2, 2], 0);\n+        doc.line(sigX + 4, y + 16, sigX + mainW - 4, y + 16);\n+        doc.setLineDashPattern([], 0);\n+    }\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+    doc.setFontSize(6.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.black);\n+    doc.text(opts.signatureName, sigX + 4, y + 21);\n+\n+    // Vertical separator\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.lightGray, 'draw');\n+    doc.setLineWidth(0.2);\n+    doc.line(sigX + mainW, y, sigX + mainW, y + rowH);\n+\n+    // Date column\n+    const dateX = sigX + mainW;\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'normal');\n+    doc.setFontSize(5.5);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.purpleGray);\n+    doc.text('DATE SIGNED', dateX + 4, y + 5);\n+\n+    doc.setFont('times', 'bold');\n+    doc.setFontSize(10);\n+    setColor(doc, BRAND.navy);\n+    doc.text(opts.date, dateX + 4, y + 15);\n+\n+    // Bottom accent line\n+    setColor(doc, opts.accentColor, 'fill');\n+    doc.rect(sigX + 4, y + 18, mainW - 8, 0.7, 'F');\n+    doc.rect(dateX + 4, y + 18, totalW - labelW - mainW - 8, 0.7, 'F');\n+}\n+\n+\n+/* ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════\n+     REPORT PDF  —  Corporate analytics summary (two pages)\n+   ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */\n+\n+export interface ReportPdfData {\n+    year: string;\n+    stats: {\n+        totalRequests: number;\n+        approved:
